 inke pita kaa naam kalyanchand yaa mehta kaalu ji tha, mata kaa naam tripta devi tha
 His sister's name was Nanaki
 inkaa vivaah solah varsh kii avasthaa main gurdaspur jile ke antargat lakhki naamak sthaan ke rahanevaale mula kii kanya sulakshani se hua tha
 He visited the country four times
 32 varsh kii avasthaa main inke pratham putr shrichand kaa janm hua
 He visited the country five times
 jise udasis kaha jaataa he, inhone kirthan ke mathyam se upadesh die
 In the last moments of his life he built his monastery on the banks of river Ravi
 aadhyatmik aadhaar par inhone apane bete ke jagah apane bhai lahana ko apana uttaradhikari banaaya
 He died in Kartarpur in 1539 AD
 nanak ne sikh dharm kii sthapana kii, nanak sufi dharm baba farid se prabhavit the
 Chaitanya Mahaprabhu - Chaitanya Mahaprabhu was born in 1486 AD in Nadia, West Bengal

 He took initiation from a monk named Keshav Bharti
 kuch log madhavendra puri ko inkaa diksha guru maanate hai
 His wife's names were Lakshmipriya and Vishnupriya
 unka dehanth urisa ke puri tirthasthal par hua
 Madvavallabhacharya - Sri Madvallabhacharya was born in 1479 AD in Champaranya
 inke pita kaa naam lakshmana bhatta or mata kaa naam yallamgaru tha

 inke do bete the-gopinath or viththalanath

 goswami tulsidas-ek mahaan kavi the
 He was born in Banda, UP
 apane jeevankaal main unhone 12 granth likhe

 inhone shriramcharitamanas kii rachana kii thi
 Dhanna- Dhanna was born into a Jat family in 1415 AD, coming from Rajputana, he became a disciple of Ramananda in Benares
 kaha jaataa he ki inhone bhagwaan kii murti ko bhojan karavaaya thadadudayaal- hindi ke bhaktikaal main gyanashrayi shakha ke pramukh sant kavi the

 inkaa sambandh dhuniya jati se he
 He left home for ten years and meditated hard
 dadu ne fatehpur sikri main akbar se bhent kii thi or chalis dinon tak aadhyatmik vishyon kii charchaa bhi karte rahe the

 inhone shabad or saakhi likhin

 32 While most states have seen an increase in crime rates over the past few years, the National Crime Records Bureau (NCRB) 2016 figures show that between 2015 and 2016 crime cases have declined in Nagaland
 2014 main, rajya main hue kul aparaadhon kii sankhya (bhartiya dand samhita or vishesh sthaneey kanoonon ke tahat panjikrut) 1,669 thi
 It increased to 1,928 in 2015
 2016 main kuch giravat dekhi gai or kul darj aparaadhon kii sankhya 1,908 rahi
 This figure has placed Nagaland at the bottom of the ncrb's list of states
 nagaland desh main teesraa sabase kam aparaadh ke maamle darj karne vaala rajya rahaa
 Only Dadra Nagar Haveli and Lakshadweep registered fewer crimes than Nagaland
 nagaland mahilaon ke prati aparaadh ko rokane ke maamle main awwal rahaa or yahaan mahilaon ke prati darj aparaadhon ke maamalon kii sankhya desh main sabase kam rahi
 However, what is worrying is that while Nagaland of course records far fewer cases of crime against women than other states, the number of crimes against women in the state has been increasing in recent years
 2014 main 68 maamle darj kiye gaye the, jabaki agle varsh yah sankhya badhkar 91 ho gai
 In 2016, 105 cases of crime against women were registered in Nagaland
 in sabhi darj maamalon main se police ne 2016 main 102 kaa nipataara kiya tha

 is tarah mahilaon ke prati aparaadhon ke liye sajaa main nagaland 41

 isse aankada bad jaataa he

 yah vishesh dasta paryatakon kii suraksha karegaa

 tandon ne ek sanyukt vaktavy main kaha, 'gramin kshetron se shahari kshetron kii ore palaayan badhane, jivan style main badlaav, adhik jaagrukta, or prabhavi chikitsa kii uplabdhta se anek maamalon main prostate cancer kii jaanch samay se hone lagi he' is beemaari kii vruddhi main ham pashchimi deshon se katai peeche nahin hai' ek hi jagah par ghanton tak baithe rahane or motaape ke kaaran bhi purushon main prostate cancer hone laga he
 ' unhone kaha, 'santrupt vasa kii adhikta vaale bhojan se prostate cancer kaa khatra paidaa ho saktaa he' prostate cancer kii surgery ke pashchaat, pashuon se praapt ucch santrupt vasa yukt bhojan lene vaale purushon main saamaanya purushon ke mukaable, yah rog hone kaa khatra doharaa ho jaataa he

 aam taur par, dawaaiyon ko mila julkar diya jaataa he taaki prostate granthi kaa aakaar badhane se roka ja sake
 It is also called combination therapy
 prostate cancer ke marijon ko ye dawaaen chah se 12 maah tak di jaati hai
 The second stage is surgery, when the cancer is spreading rapidly

 ) kings ilevan punjab ne ajahar mahmud (80) or shaan marsh (63) ke ardhshtakon ke baad kasi gendbaaji se shanivaar ko indian premier lig tii-20 match main sheersh par chal rahi mumbai indiens ko 50 ran se parajeet kiya
 After getting the batting invitation, Punjab's team started with Mahmood and Marsh 14 despite a poor start
 2 over main tisare wicket ke liye 148 ran kii bhagidaari se aath wicket par 183 ran kaa sammanjanak score khadaa karne main safal rahi
 Mahmud hit eight fours and four sixes in a 44-ball innings while Marsh hit 11 fours in a 47-ball innings
 mumbai indiens iske jawaab main 19
 Only scored 133 runs in 1 over
 uske liye ambaati rayudu 26 ran banaakar sheersh scorer rahe jabaki captain rohit sharma ne 25, salaami ballebaaj aditya taare ne 22 or kiron pollard ne 22 or rishi dhawan ne 14 ran banaaye
 The Mumbai Indians lost the final match to slip from the top to the second position, winning 11 of 16 matches and losing five
 uske 22 ank hai
 Preity Zinta's team Punjab finished their campaign in 16 matches with six points from six
 kings ilevan punjab ke liye piyush chawla ne 20 ran, sandip sharma ne 30 ran or mahmud ne 24 ran dekar do do wicket praapt kiye jabaki praveen kumaar, parvinder awana or adam gilcrist ke naam ek-ek wicket rahaa
 Playing his last IPL match, Kings XI Punjab captain Gilchrist decided to bowl the last over of the match and interestingly, he also took the wicket of Harbhajan Singh (05) on its first ball
 phir gendbaaji ke dauraan chotil hue dhaval kulkarni ballebaaji ke liye nahin utre jisase kings ilevan punjab ne paanch gend rahete jeet darj kii
 Mahmood was awarded the 'man of the match' for his all-round performance after taking a half-century inning
 play of kii daud se pehle hi baahar ho chuki punjab ke ballebaaj marsh or mahmud ne chauke or chakke jamaakar mumbai indiens ke gendbaajon kii dhajjiyaan uda di
 The team had lost two wickets for six runs in the third over
 in donon khilaadiyon main mahmud zyada aakraamak the, jinhone ek over main 10 se zyada ran banaae
 Manan Vohra finally scored an unbeaten 20-run eight-ball eight
 mumbai indiens ke liye lasith malinga ne 39 ran dekar teen wicket jabaki nathan colter nil, rishi dhawan, harbhajan or kirone pollard ne ek-ek wicket liya
 Punjab started badly, with openers Mandeep Singh (01) and Adam Gilchrist (05) reaching the dressing room by the third over, when the score was just six runs
 mandeep ne rishi dhawan kii gend ko samaj nahin sake or duusare over main mid of par pollard ko sidhaa kaich de baithe
 Gilchrist bowled to Coulter Neil in the third over
 do jhatkon se punjab kii ballebaaji ko dhimaa kar diya lekin marsh or mahmud ne dhire-dhire isamen sudhaar karnaa shuru kiya
 Marsh started aggression by scoring three fours in the sixth over of Dhawal Kulkarni, while Mahmood washed Malinga for a six and three fours off consecutive balls and scored 20 runs in the eighth over
 punjab ne 10 over ke baad do wicket par 80 ran bana liye the
 In the 13th over, Mahmood hit two consecutive sixes and a four off Glenn Maxwell
 agle over main jab vah 50 ran par the to colter nil ne unka kaich chhod diya
 The comments marsh ko bhi harbhajan singh ne isi over main jeevandaan diya, tab vah 54 ran ke score par the
 This Australian was dismissed by Harbhajan in the 17th over
 iske baad mahmud bhi malinga kii gend par pagabaadha out ho gayi
 David Miller (06), Gurkirat Singh (00), Piyush Chawla (01) and Praveen Kumar (00) also did not last long
 ballebaaji kaa nyauta milane ke baad punjab kii team kharaab shuruyaat ke baavjood mahmud or marsh ne 14
 a partnership of 148 runs for the third wicket in 2 overs, managed to score a respectable score of 183 for eight
 mahmud ne 44 gend kii pari main aath chauke or chaar chakke jade jabaki marsh ne 47 gend kii pari main 11 chauke jamaaye
 Mumbai Indians 19 in response to this
 1 over main 133 ran hi bana saki
 For him, Ambati Rayudu was the top scorer with 26 runs, while captain Rohit Sharma scored 25, opener Aditya Tare 22 and Kirron Pollard 22 and Rishi Dhawan 14
 mumbai indiens kii team antim match main haar se sheersh se duusare sthaan par khisak gayi, usne 16 maichon main 11 jeet darj kii or paanch main use shikast mili
 It has 22 digits
 priti jinta kii team punjab ne apana abhiyaan 16 maichon main 16 ank se chathe sthaan par samaapt kiya
 For Kings XI Punjab, Piyush Chawla took 20 wickets, Sandeep Sharma 30 runs and Mahmood took two wickets for 24 runs while Praveen Kumar, Parvinder Awana and Adam Gilchrist had one wicket each
 apana antim ipel main match khel rahe kings ilevan punjab ke captain gilcrist ne match kaa antim over gendbaaji karne kaa faisla kiya or dilachasp baat yah rahi ki unhone isaki pehali gend par harbhajan singh (05) kaa wicket bhi jhatak liya
 Then Dhawal Kulkarni, who was injured during the bowling, did not come out to bat, so that Kings XI Punjab won with five balls
 mahmud ko ardhshtkeey pari khilne ke baad do wicket hasil kar oleround pradarshan karne ke liye ‘main aaf da match’ se nawaja gaya
 Punjab batsmen Marsh and Mehmood, who were already out before the play-off race, blasted the Mumbai Indians bowlers with fours and sixes
 team ne tisare over main chah ran par do wicket kho die the
 Mahmud was the more aggressive of these two players, scoring more than 10 runs in an over
 manan vohara ne ant main aath gend main naabad 20 ran kii pari kheli
 For Mumbai Indians, Lasith Malinga took three wickets for 39 runs while Nathan Coulter Neil, Rishi Dhawan, Harbhajan and Kieron Pollard took one wicket each
 punjab kii shuruyaat kaaphi kharaab rahi, salaami ballebaaj mandeep singh (01) or adam gilcrist (05) tisare over tak dressing room pahunch gayi, tab score keval chah ran tha
 Mandeep could not understand Rishi Dhawan's ball and was caught by Pollard at mid-off in the second over
 gilcrist tisare over main colter nil kii gend par bold ho gayi
 Punjab's batting was slowed down by two aftershocks but Marsh and Mahmud slowly began to improve
 marsh ne dhaval kulkarni ke chathe over main teen chauke jamaakar aakraamakata kii shuruyaat kii jabaki mahmud ne lagaataar gendon par ek chakka or teen chauke jamaakar malinga ko dhoyaa or aathven over main 20 ran jutaye
 Punjab had scored 80 runs for two wickets after 10 overs
 mahmud ne 13wein over main glen maxwell par lagaataar gend main do chakke or ek chaukaa jamaaya
 In the next over when he was on 50, Coulter Neil dropped his catch
 tippaniyan Marsh was also given life by Harbhajan Singh in this over, when he was on a score of 54 runs
 yah australian 17wein over main harbhajan kii gend par out hua
 After this, Mahmud was lbw to Malinga
 david miller (06), gurkirat singh (00), piyush chawla (01) or praveen kumaar (00) bhi zyada der tak nahin tike

 padhie, saat samandar paar barsilona main quality bitaa rahe hai 'good frends' deepika padukon or ranvirdilachasp baat yah he ki jab deepika ne turki jane kaa man banaaya to ek cosmetic brands unase naaraaz ho gaya

 isse cosmetic brands naaraaz ho gaya, kyonki pehle bahut mushkil se deepika se shooting dats milin thi

 team india ke purv captain emes dhoni ipel 10 main kings XI punjab ke kilaaf indore main bhale hi balle se jalawaa nahin dikhaa sake lekin unhone T20 cricket main ek nayaa record apane naam kar liya

 maahi bharat kii ore se sabase zyada tii20 match khilne vaale khilaadi hai
 The match against Punjab is the 250th match of his T20 cricket career
 tippaniyan The 35-year-old Dhoni played T20 cricket for the first time in 2006 under the captaincy of Virender Sehwag in Johannesburg
 ve is match main zero par out hue the lekin unhone ek kaich or ek ran out kiya

 2007 main dhoni kii apni captaini main bharat ne dakshin africa main hue pehle T20 world cap main champion banaaya

 iske alaava 4 baar chennai ipel main upavijeta bhi rahi

 Dhoni is at number 13 in this list

 On the other hand, T20 cricket batsman Chris Gayle has scored 9969 runs in 287 matches with 18 centuries
 dhoni is list main 13wein number par hai
 According to intelligence reports, Naxalite organizations can also target big cities like Delhi for their attacks in the coming months as they are looking for opportunities to spread violence on a large scale
 khufia agenciyon dwaara taiyaar kii gai is report ke anusaar, antarrashtriya str par logon kaa dhyaan khinchne or apane caderon kaa hausala badhaane ke lihaaj se adhik se adhik phayda hasil karne kii koshish main naksali ab bade paimaane par hinsa failaane kii koshish karenge or shahari ilaakon main aasaani se shikaar banaae ja sakane vaale logon ko nishane par lenge
 The report said that after the killing of 27 people, including Congress leaders in Chhattisgarh, the Naxalites have increased significantly, and now they want to expand the activities even outside their sphere of influence and consider killing targets as an important option
 
 report main kaha gaya he ki darasal, maovadiyon ko haal ke samay main kaaphi nuksaan jhelana pada he or jagadalpur main 25 may (shanivaar) ko kiya gaya hamalaa maovadiyon kii rashtriya str par charchaa main aane kii koshishon kaa parinaam tha
 Along with this, they also wanted to reestablish their influence on the people living in the places where they were present
 sarkari sutron ne kaha ki maovadiyon kii niraashaa kaa andaja unke sheersh netaaon ke bich hui baatcheet ko sunakar lagaaya ja saktaa he
 In fact, security agencies have heard conversations between some top Maoists leaders who are hiding in the thick forests of Chhattisgarh, Jharkhand and Odisha
 suraksha agenciyon kaa maananaa he ki maovadiyon ke khilaaf karrwai ek dirghakaalik lakshya he, or iske liye ardhsainik balon ke 27 hajaar javaanon kii or zarurat padegi
 It will take at least two to three years for their elimination from Naxalite affected areas in Bastar (chhattisgarh), Malkangiri, Koraput (odisha) and Latehar (jharkhand)
 is samay naksal-virdohi abhiyaanon main ardhsainik balon ke 82 hajaar jawan tainaat hai
 Apart from this, soldiers of state police forces also participate in these operations
 sutron ne kaha ki madhya or purvi bharat main kai ilaake hai, jahaan prashasan naam kii koi cheez nahin he or police bhi atyant kam sankhya main tainaat he
 Naxalites are taking advantage of this situation
 sutron ne bataaya ki bastar kshetra main, jo kerala rajya ke baraabar kshetrafal vaala he, keval 18 hajaar suraksha jawan tainaat hai, jo katai naakaafi hai
 The comments suraksha bal cobra or andhra pradesh ke grehounds jaise vishisht balon ko shaamil kar naksaliyon ke khilaaf nirnaayak abhiyaan kii taiyaari kar rahe hai, aise main khufia jaankaree par aadhaarit abhiyaan nikat bhavishya main ho sakate hai
 As part of the new strategy, search operations will be carried out in Chhattisgarh, Jharkhand and Odisha with the help of Unmanned Aerial Vehicles (uavs) and then attacked from several locations using security forces including special forces
 sutron ne kaha ki nai ranneeti ke tahat pehle naksaliyon ke niyantran vaale ilaakon par kabja kiya jayega or phir vahiin se surakshabalon kaa abhiyaan sanchalit kiya jayega
 According to this report prepared by the intelligence agencies, the Naxalites will now try to spread violence on a large scale in urban areas in an attempt to gain maximum attention in order to grab the attention of international people and encourage their cadres
 Will easily target people who can be hunted
 report main kaha gaya ki chhattisgarh main congress netaaon sahit 27 logon kii hatya ke baad naksaliyon kaa hausala kaaphi bad gaya he, or ab ve apane prabhavakshetra ke baahar bhi gatividhiyon kaa vistaar karnaa chaahate hai or nishane tay kar hatyaein karne ko mahatvapurn vikalp maan rahe hai
 The report said that in fact, the Maoists have suffered a lot in recent times and the attack on May 25 (saturday) in Jagdalpur was the result of the Maoists' attempts to come to national discussion
 iske saath hi ve apni upasthiti vaali jagahon par rah rahe logon par bhi apane prabhaav ko phir sthapit karnaa chaahate the
 Government sources said that the Maoists' disappointment can be gauged from the conversations between their top leaders
 darasal, suraksha agenciyon ne maovadiyon ke kuch sheersh netaaon ke bich hone vaali baatcheet suni he, jo chhattisgarh, jharkhand or odisha ke ghaney jangalon main chhipe hue hai
 Security agencies believe that action against the Maoists is a long-term goal, and 27,000 paramilitary personnel will be needed for this
 bastar (chhattisgarh), malkangiri, koraput (odisha) or lateher (jharkhand) main naksaliyon ke prabhaav vaale ilaakon se unke safaye main kam se kam do se teen saal lagenge
 At present, 82,000 paramilitary personnel are deployed in anti-naxal operations
 iske alaava rajya police balon ke jawan bhi in abhiyaanon main shaamil hote hai
 Sources said that there are many areas in central and eastern India, where there is no such thing as administration and police are also deployed in very small numbers
 naksali isi sthiti kaa phayda uthaa rahe hai
 Sources said that in the Bastar region, which is equivalent to the state of Kerala, only 18,000 security personnel are deployed, who are absolutely insufficient
 tippaniyan The security forces are preparing for a decisive campaign against the Naxalites by involving specific forces like Cobra and Greyhounds of Andhra Pradesh, so intelligence-based operations may take place in the near future
 nai ranneeti ke tahat chhattisgarh, jharkhand or odisha main maanavrahit hawaii yaan (yuavi) kii madad se pehle talaashi abhiyaan chalaaya jayega or phir vishesh balon sahit suraksha balon kaa upyog kar kai sthanon se hamalaa bolaa jayega
 Sources said that under the new strategy, the areas controlled by Naxalites will be captured first and then the operations of security forces will be conducted from there
